                        <span class="ph" id="DDCCleanDef"
                            ><a name="DDCCleanDef" data-id=""><!-- --></a
                            >Indicates the record’s clean status as compared
                            with Data.com. Values are:
                            <samp class="ph systemoutput">Matched</samp>,
                            <samp class="ph systemoutput">Different</samp>,
                            <samp class="ph systemoutput">Acknowledged</samp>,
                            <samp class="ph systemoutput">NotFound</samp>,
                            <samp class="ph systemoutput">Inactive</samp>,
                            <samp class="ph systemoutput">Pending</samp>,<samp
                                class="ph systemoutput"
                            >
                                SelectMatch</samp
                            >, or
                            <samp class="ph systemoutput">Skipped</samp></span
                        >.
                        <div class="p">
                            Several values for
                            <span class="keyword parmname">CleanStatus</span>
                            display with different labels on the account record
                            detail page.
                            <ul class="ul bulletList">
                                <li class="li">
                                    <samp class="ph systemoutput">Matched</samp>
                                    displays as
                                    <samp class="ph systemoutput">In Sync</samp>
                                </li>

                                <li class="li">
                                    <samp class="ph systemoutput"
                                        >Acknowledged</samp
                                    >
                                    displays as
                                    <samp class="ph systemoutput"
                                        >Reviewed</samp
                                    >
                                </li>

                                <li class="li">
                                    <samp class="ph systemoutput">Pending</samp>
                                    displays as
                                    <samp class="ph systemoutput"
                                        >Not Compared</samp
                                    >
                                </li>
                            </ul>
                        </div>
                    </dd>
                </dl>
            </td>

        <tr>
            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e115" data-title="Field Name">
                <span class="keyword parmname" id="DunsNumber"
                    ><a name="DunsNumber" data-id=""><!-- --></a
                    >DunsNumber</span
                >
            </td>

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e118" data-title="Details">
                <dl class="dl detailList">
                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Type</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">string</dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Properties</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Create, Filter, Group, Nillable, Sort, Update
                    </dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Description</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        <span class="ph" id="DunsNoDef"
                            ><a name="DunsNoDef" data-id=""><!-- --></a>The Data
                            Universal Numbering System (D-U-N-S) number is a
                            unique, nine-digit number assigned to every business
                            location in the Dun &amp; Bradstreet database that
                            has a unique, separate, and distinct operation.
                            D-U-N-S numbers are used by industries and
                            organizations around the world as a global standard
                            for business identification and tracking. Maximum
                            size is 9 characters.</span
                        >
                        This field is available on business accounts, not person
                        accounts.
                        <div class="box message info">
                            <doc-content-callout
                                ><p>
                                    <span class="ph" id="DdccApiNote"
                                        ><a name="DdccApiNote" data-id=""
                                            ><!-- --></a
                                        >This field is only available to
                                        organizations that use Data.com
                                        Prospector or Data.com Clean.</span
                                    >
                                </p></doc-content-callout
                            >
                        </div>
                    </dd>
                </dl>
            </td>
        </tr>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Properties</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Defaulted on create, Filter, Group, Sort, Update
                    </dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Description</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Indicates whether the account has at least one contact
                        enabled to use the org's Customer Portal (<samp
                            class="codeph nolang"
                            >true</samp
                        >) or not (<samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>).
                        This field is available if Customer Portal is enabled OR
                        digital experiences is enabled and you have Customer
                        Portal licenses.
                        <p class="p">
                            If your org is enabled to use Content Security
                            Policy (CSP) features, then this field is visible on
                            the Account object even if those features are later
                            disabled.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            If you change this field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            disable up to 100 Customer Portal users associated
                            with the account and permanently delete all of the
                            account's Customer Portal roles and groups. You
                            can't restore deleted Customer Portal roles and
                            groups.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            This field can be updated in API version 16.0 and
                            later.
                        </p>
                        <div class="box message confirm">
                            <doc-content-callout
                                ><p>
                                    We recommend that you update up to 50
                                    contacts simultaneously when changing the
                                    accounts on contacts enabled for a Customer
                                    Portal or partner portal. We also recommend
                                    that you make this update after business
                                    hours.
                                </p></doc-content-callout
                            >
                        </div>
                    </dd>
                </dl>
            </td>
        </tr>

                                    including report filters, list view filters,

                                    SOQL query returns person accounts with
                                    birthdays later in the year than today:
                                </p>
                                <div class="codeSection soql" lwc:dom="manual">

                            ></doc-content-callout>

                    </dd>
                </dl>

                            location in the Dun &amp; Bradstreet database that
                            has a unique, separate, and distinct operation.

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e118" data-title="Details">

                        Indicates whether the account has at least one contact
                        enabled to use the org's Customer Portal (<samp
                            class="codeph nolang"
                            >true</samp
                        >) or not (<samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>).
                        This field is available if Customer Portal is enabled OR
                        digital experiences is enabled and you have Customer
                        Portal licenses.
                        <p class="p">
                            If your org is enabled to use Content Security
                            Policy (CSP) features, then this field is visible on
                            the Account object even if those features are later
                            disabled.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            If you change this field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            disable up to 100 Customer Portal users associated
                            with the account and permanently delete all of the
                            account's Customer Portal roles and groups. You
                            can't restore deleted Customer Portal roles and
                            groups.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            This field can be updated in API version 16.0 and
                            later.
                        </p>
                        <div class="box message confirm">
                            <doc-content-callout
                                ><p>
                                    We recommend that you update up to 50
                                    contacts simultaneously when changing the
                                    accounts on contacts enabled for a Customer
                                    Portal or partner portal. We also recommend
                                    that you make this update after business
                                    hours.
                                </p></doc-content-callout
                            >
                        </div>
                    </dd>
                </dl>
            </td>
        </tr>

                >
            </td>

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e118" data-title="Details">
                <dl class="dl detailList">
                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Type</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">boolean</dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Properties</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Defaulted on create, Filter, Group, Sort, Update
                    </dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Description</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Indicates whether the account has at least one contact
                        enabled to use the org's partner portal (<samp
                            class="codeph nolang"
                            >true</samp
                        >) or not (<samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>).
                        This field is available if partner relationship
                        management (partner portal) is enabled ORdigitial
                        experiences is enabled and you have partner portal
                        licenses.
                        <p class="p">
                            If you change this field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            disable up to 15 partner portal users associated
                            with the account and permanently delete all of the
                            account's partner portal roles and groups. You can't
                            restore deleted partner portal roles and groups.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            Disabling a partner portal user in the Salesforce
                            user interface or the API does not change this
                            field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            Even if this field's value is
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            enable a contact on an account as a partner portal
                            user via the API.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            <span class="ph" id="Ver16Update"
                                ><a name="Ver16Update" data-id=""><!-- --></a
                                >This field can be updated in API version 16.0
                                and later.</span
                            >
                        </p>
                        <div class="box message confirm">
                            <doc-content-callout
                                ><p>
                                    We recommend that you update up to 50
                                    contacts simultaneously when changing the
                                    accounts on contacts enabled for a Customer
                                    Portal or partner portal. We also recommend
                                    that you make this update after business
                                    hours.
                                </p></doc-content-callout
                            >
                        </div>
                    </dd>
                </dl>
            </td>
        </tr>

                            depending on your version of the API:

                            ><a name="DunsNoDef" data-id=""><!-- --></a>The Data
                            Universal Numbering System (D-U-N-S) number is a
                            unique, nine-digit number assigned to every business
                            location in the Dun &amp; Bradstreet database that
                            has a unique, separate, and distinct operation.
                            D-U-N-S numbers are used by industries and
                            organizations around the world as a global standard
                            for business identification and tracking. Maximum
                            size is 9 characters.</span
                        >
                        This field is available on business accounts, not person
                        accounts.

                                        Prospector or Data.com Clean.</span
                                    >

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e115" data-title="Field Name">
                <span class="keyword parmname" id="iscustomerportal"
                    ><a name="iscustomerportal" data-id=""><!-- --></a
                    >IsCustomerPortal</span
                >
            </td>

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e118" data-title="Details">
                <dl class="dl detailList">
                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Type</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">boolean</dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Properties</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Defaulted on create, Filter, Group, Sort, Update
                    </dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Description</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Indicates whether the account has at least one contact
                        enabled to use the org's Customer Portal (<samp
                            class="codeph nolang"
                            >true</samp
                        >) or not (<samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>).
                        This field is available if Customer Portal is enabled OR
                        digital experiences is enabled and you have Customer
                        Portal licenses.
                        <p class="p">
                            If your org is enabled to use Content Security
                            Policy (CSP) features, then this field is visible on
                            the Account object even if those features are later
                            disabled.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            If you change this field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            disable up to 100 Customer Portal users associated
                            with the account and permanently delete all of the
                            account's Customer Portal roles and groups. You
                            can't restore deleted Customer Portal roles and
                            groups.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            This field can be updated in API version 16.0 and
                            later.
                        </p>
                        <div class="box message confirm">
                            <doc-content-callout
                                ><p>
                                    We recommend that you update up to 50
                                    contacts simultaneously when changing the
                                    accounts on contacts enabled for a Customer
                                    Portal or partner portal. We also recommend
                                    that you make this update after business
                                    hours.
                                </p></doc-content-callout
                            >
                        </div>
                    </dd>
                </dl>
            </td>
        </tr>

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e115" data-title="Field Name">

                >
            </td>

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e118" data-title="Details">
                <dl class="dl detailList">
                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Type</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">boolean</dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Properties</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Defaulted on create, Filter, Group, Sort, Update
                    </dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Description</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Indicates whether the account has at least one contact
                        enabled to use the org's partner portal (<samp
                            class="codeph nolang"
                            >true</samp
                        >) or not (<samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>).
                        This field is available if partner relationship
                        management (partner portal) is enabled ORdigitial
                        experiences is enabled and you have partner portal
                        licenses.
                        <p class="p">
                            If you change this field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            disable up to 15 partner portal users associated
                            with the account and permanently delete all of the
                            account's partner portal roles and groups. You can't
                            restore deleted partner portal roles and groups.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            Disabling a partner portal user in the Salesforce
                            user interface or the API does not change this
                            field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            Even if this field's value is
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            enable a contact on an account as a partner portal
                            user via the API.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            <span class="ph" id="Ver16Update"
                                ><a name="Ver16Update" data-id=""><!-- --></a
                                >This field can be updated in API version 16.0
                                and later.</span
                            >
                        </p>
                        <div class="box message confirm">
                            <doc-content-callout
                                ><p>
                                    We recommend that you update up to 50
                                    contacts simultaneously when changing the
                                    accounts on contacts enabled for a Customer
                                    Portal or partner portal. We also recommend
                                    that you make this update after business
                                    hours.
                                </p></doc-content-callout
                            >
                        </div>

                        <p class="p">
                            If you have set up account teams in your org,
                            updating this field has different consequences
                            depending on your version of the API:
                        </p>
                        <a name="sharing_bug_fix_179899" data-id=""><!-- --></a>
                        <ul class="ul bulletList" id="sharing_bug_fix_179899">
                            <li class="li">
                                For API version 12.0 and later, sharing records
                                are kept, as they are for all objects.
                            </li>

                            <li class="li">
                                For API version before 12.0, sharing records are
                                deleted.
                            </li>

                            <li class="li">
                                For API version 16.0 and later, users must have
                                the “Transfer Record” permission in order to
                                update (transfer) account ownership using this
                                field.

                            unique, nine-digit number assigned to every business
                            location in the Dun &amp; Bradstreet database that
                            has a unique, separate, and distinct operation.
                            D-U-N-S numbers are used by industries and
                            organizations around the world as a global standard
                            for business identification and tracking. Maximum

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e115" data-title="Field Name">
                <span class="keyword parmname" id="iscustomerportal"
                    ><a name="iscustomerportal" data-id=""><!-- --></a
                    >IsCustomerPortal</span
                >
            </td>

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e118" data-title="Details">
                <dl class="dl detailList">
                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Type</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">boolean</dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Properties</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Defaulted on create, Filter, Group, Sort, Update
                    </dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Description</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Indicates whether the account has at least one contact
                        enabled to use the org's Customer Portal (<samp
                            class="codeph nolang"
                            >true</samp
                        >) or not (<samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>).
                        This field is available if Customer Portal is enabled OR
                        digital experiences is enabled and you have Customer
                        Portal licenses.
                        <p class="p">
                            If your org is enabled to use Content Security
                            Policy (CSP) features, then this field is visible on
                            the Account object even if those features are later
                            disabled.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            If you change this field's value from
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">true</samp> to
                            <samp class="codeph nolang">false</samp>, you can
                            disable up to 100 Customer Portal users associated
                            with the account and permanently delete all of the
                            account's Customer Portal roles and groups. You
                            can't restore deleted Customer Portal roles and
                            groups.
                        </p>
                        <p class="p">
                            This field can be updated in API version 16.0 and
                            later.
                        </p>
                        <div class="box message confirm">
                            <doc-content-callout
                                ><p>
                                    We recommend that you update up to 50
                                    contacts simultaneously when changing the
                                    accounts on contacts enabled for a Customer
                                    Portal or partner portal. We also recommend
                                    that you make this update after business
                                    hours.
                                </p></doc-content-callout
                            >
                        </div>
                    </dd>
                </dl>
            </td>
        </tr>

                            user via the API.

        <tr>
            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e115" data-title="Field Name">
                <span class="keyword parmname" id="JigsawField"
                    ><a name="JigsawField" data-id=""><!-- --></a>Jigsaw</span
                >
            </td>

            <td class="entry" headers="d23861e118" data-title="Details">
                <dl class="dl detailList">
                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Type</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">string</dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Properties</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        Create, Filter, Group, Nillable, Sort, Update
                    </dd>

                    <dt class="dt dlterm">Description</dt>

                    <dd class="dd">
                        References the ID of a company in Data.com. If an
                        account has a value in this field, it means that the
                        account was imported from Data.com. If the field value
                        is <samp class="codeph nolang">null</samp>, the account
                        was not imported from Data.com. Maximum size is 20
                        characters. Available in API version 22.0 and later.
                        Label is <strong class="ph b">Data.com Key</strong>.
                        This field is available on business accounts, not person
                        accounts.

                        <p class="p">
                            If you have set up account teams in your org,
                            updating this field has different consequences
                            depending on your version of the API:
                        </p>

                        <ul class="ul bulletList" id="sharing_bug_fix_179899">
                            <li class="li">
                                For API version 12.0 and later, sharing records
                                are kept, as they are for all objects.
                            </li>

                            <li class="li">
                                For API version before 12.0, sharing records are
                                deleted.
                            </li>

                            <li class="li">
                                For API version 16.0 and later, users must have
                                the “Transfer Record” permission in order to
                                update (transfer) account ownership using this
                                field.

                        for details on geolocation compound fields.

                    </dd>
